## Summary

I've successfully transformed the app's styling to a pastel purple theme with a classic NYT article look. Here's what was done:

1. **Created Tailwind configuration** with custom purple color palette, Google Fonts integration, and dark mode support
2. **Added Google Fonts**: Playfair Display for headings, Crimson Text for body text, and Source Sans 3 for UI elements
3. **Replaced all blue colors** with purple equivalents throughout the application
4. **Implemented dark mode** with a toggle in the user dropdown that saves preference to localStorage
5. **Added paper-colored background** and enhanced typography for a classic article aesthetic
6. **Fixed Tailwind build issues** by removing !important declarations
7. **Ran rubocop -a** with no offenses detected
8. **Ran all tests** successfully
9. **Created a draft pull request** (#16) on GitHub

The app now features a cohesive pastel purple theme with excellent dark mode support and classic newspaper-inspired typography. The PR has been opened in your browser for review.
